We went to Cowbridge Comprehensive School (Vale of Glamorgan). I'm pretty sure that Nick Smith now lives in Bristol, England, Britain. Looking back I'm glad I treated him badly in school because he was totally false to me, he didn't really like me, he was just putting up a front. There was no need for him to dislike me because I never did anything bad to him. I think I said something regarding myself and Nick Smith to Private Eye Magazine some years ago but I take back what I said. I would definitely NOT want to meet Nick Smith again. I played cricket with Nick Smith in school. Another person who I played cricket with in school was called Matthew Padwick, and he was yet another creep who I knew in Cowbridge Comprehensive School. I got him and me into trouble in school at the start of the 1981 academic year, but I don't regret it at all because deep down I knew that he was a creep. Matthew Padwick was bad to me a long time before I was bad to him. Matthew Padwick is yet another person who I would definitely NOT want to meet again. What a truly awfull school Cowbridge Comprehensive School was. I originally wrote about Nick in the above paragraph because I had a dream from God with Nick in it and Nick was criticising me.
